#!/usr/bin/env bash
# Usage: lfphp-get openssl [1.1.1] [--compile]
export COMPILE=0
# this needs to change!
export bin_source="http://opensource.unlikelysource.com"
cd
if [[ -z "$1" ]]; then
    read -r -p "Which version of OpenSSL do you wish to install? (1.1.1) " response
else
    response=$1
fi
if [[ "$response" != "1\.1\.1" ]]; then
	export src_root="OpenSSL_1_1_1g"
else
    echo -e "SORRY! Only these versions are currently supported: 1.1.1 . ABORTING..."
    exit 2
fi
if [[ ! -z "$2" && "$2" == "--compile" ]]; then
    COMPILE=1
fi
if [[ "$COMPILE" -gt 0 ]]; then
	cd /tmp
	export src_source="https://github.com/openssl/openssl/archive/"$src_root".zip"
	wget -O openssl.zip $src_source
	if [[ ! -f openssl.zip ]]; then
	  echo -e "OpenSSL zip file not found.  Aborting!"
	  echo ""
	  exit 1
	fi
	unzip openssl.zip
	cd /tmp/openssl-$src_root
	./config -Wl,-rpath=/usr/lib64 --prefix=/usr --openssldir=/usr
	make
	make install
	cd /tmp
	rm /tmp/openssl.zip
	rm -rf /tmp/openssl-$src_root
	if [[ $? -gt 0 ]]; then
	  echo -e "OpenSSL Compilation ERROR!  Aborting!"
	  echo ""
	  exit 1
	fi
else
	cd /
	wget $bin_source/$src_root.zip
	# unzip
	unzip -o $src_root.zip
	mkdir /usr/private
	mkdir /usr/certs	
	# create new symlinks
	ln -s -f /usr/lib/libcrypto.so.1.1 /usr/lib/libcrypto.so
	ln -s -f /usr/lib/libssl.so.1.1 /usr/lib/libssl.so
	ln -s -f /usr/share/man/man3/ADMISSIONS.3 /usr/share/man/man3/ADMISSIONS_get0_admissionAuthority.3
